        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          margin: auto;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          position: sticky;

          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





A portal adopting a portal predecessor selected in a nested <selectmenu> causes UaF.



<span class="line"><!---->A portal adopting a portal predecessor selected in a nested &lt;selectmenu&gt; causes UaF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 110.0.5475.0



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 110.0.5475.0<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. python3 -m http.server 9000



<span class="line"><!---->1. python3 -m http.server 9000<!----></span>



<br>





2. chrome --enable-features=Portals --enable-experimental-web-platform-features



<span class="line"><!---->2. chrome --enable-features=Portals --enable-experimental-web-platform-features<!----></span>



<br>





3. Open DevTools



<span class="line"><!---->3. Open DevTools<!----></span>



<br>





4. Open 



<span class="line"><!---->4. Open <!----></span>





http://localhost:9000/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:9000/poc.html"><!---->http://localhost:9000/poc.html<!----></a>

This occurs if:



<span class="line"><!---->This occurs if:<!----></span>



<br>





- In the previous frame, the AnchorScrollData object has a scroller



<span class="line"><!---->- In the previous frame, the AnchorScrollData object has a scroller<!----></span>



<br>





- In the next frame, the scroller is gone, and there's something else triggering a paint update on the anchor-positioned element



<span class="line"><!---->- In the next frame, the scroller is gone, and there's something else triggering a paint update on the anchor-positioned element<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Not sure if this is the root cause of this UaF, but I'll fix the DCHECK hit first anyways.

I figured it out.



<span class="line"><!---->I figured it out.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The uaf object is created and freed at property_tree.cc:79:



<span class="line"><!---->The uaf object is created and freed at property_tree.cc:79:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





template <typename T>



<span class="line"><!---->template &lt;typename T&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





int PropertyTree<T>::Insert(const T& tree_node, int parent_id) {



<span class="line"><!---->int PropertyTree&lt;T&gt;::Insert(const T&amp; tree_node, int parent_id) {<!----></span>



<br>





  DCHECK_GT(nodes_.size(), 0u);



<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK_GT(nodes_.size(), 0u);<!----></span>



<br>





  nodes_.push_back(tree_node);  <---



<span class="line"><!---->  nodes_.push_back(tree_node);  &lt;---<!----></span>



<br>





  T& node = nodes_.back();



<span class="line"><!---->  T&amp; node = nodes_.back();<!----></span>



<br>





  node.parent_id = parent_id;



<span class="line"><!---->  node.parent_id = parent_id;<!----></span>



<br>





  node.id = static_cast<int>(nodes_.size()) - 1;



<span class="line"><!---->  node.id = static_cast&lt;int&gt;(nodes_.size()) - 1;<!----></span>



<br>





  return node.id;



<span class="line"><!---->  return node.id;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





And the use-after-free is at compositing/property_tree_manager.cc:469



<span class="line"><!---->And the use-after-free is at compositing/property_tree_manager.cc:469<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





  auto compositor_element_id = transform_node.GetCompositorElementId();



<span class="line"><!---->  auto compositor_element_id = transform_node.GetCompositorElementId();<!----></span>



<br>





  if (compositor_element_id) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (compositor_element_id) {<!----></span>



<br>





    transform_tree_.SetElementIdForNodeId(id, compositor_element_id);



<span class="line"><!---->    transform_tree_.SetElementIdForNodeId(id, compositor_element_id);<!----></span>



<br>





    compositor_node.element_id = compositor_element_id;  <---



<span class="line"><!---->    compositor_node.element_id = compositor_element_id;  &lt;---<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Here we are holding |compositor_node| as a reference to a vector entry, but the vector can be reallocated in the previous EnsureCompositorScrollNode call at L458/460, leaving |compositor_node| reference invalid.



<span class="line"><!---->Here we are holding |compositor_node| as a reference to a vector entry, but the vector can be reallocated in the previous EnsureCompositorScrollNode call at L458/460, leaving |compositor_node| reference invalid.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Sticky positioning does the same but is safe from this issue, because it only calls EnsureCompositorScrollNode for an ancestor node, so at this time the scroll node should have already been created.



<span class="line"><!---->Sticky positioning does the same but is safe from this issue, because it only calls EnsureCompositorScrollNode for an ancestor node, so at this time the scroll node should have already been created.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Anchor positioning does that for a node in a different subtree, and causes this issue.



<span class="line"><!---->Anchor positioning does that for a node in a different subtree, and causes this issue.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





So the uaf bug is unrelated to this patch, and the right fix should be to change |compositor_node| into a ptr and revalidate it after EnsureCompositorScrollNode calls.



<span class="line"><!---->So the uaf bug is unrelated to this patch, and the right fix should be to change |compositor_node| into a ptr and revalidate it after EnsureCompositorScrollNode calls.<!----></span>

Author: Xiaocheng Hu <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Xiaocheng Hu &lt;<!----></span>





xiaochengh@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/xiaochengh@chromium.org"><!---->xiaochengh@chromium.org<!----></a>

Date: Tue Jan 10 02:33:12 2023



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue Jan 10 02:33:12 2023<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[anchor-position] Always use compositor scroller ids for composited scrolling



<span class="line"><!---->[anchor-position] Always use compositor scroller ids for composited scrolling<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The existing implementation for composited scrolling is problematic



<span class="line"><!---->The existing implementation for composited scrolling is problematic<!----></span>



<br>





because if scrollers have changed in a style update, then it might



<span class="line"><!---->because if scrollers have changed in a style update, then it might<!----></span>



<br>





access data that is stale or already gone in the subsequent paint



<span class="line"><!---->access data that is stale or already gone in the subsequent paint<!----></span>



<br>





property tree building.



<span class="line"><!---->property tree building.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This patch basically follows the outline in

Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
